-- =============================================================================
-- [ 전용 블랙리스트 탭 생성 및 실시간 알림 시스템 ]
-- =============================================================================


local ChatBlacklist = {}
local BlacklistUIElements = {}

local function RefreshBlacklistUI()
    for _, element in ipairs(BlacklistUIElements) do
        pcall(function() element:Destroy() end)
    end
    table.clear(BlacklistUIElements)

    local titleLabel = BlacklistTab:CreateLabel("📜 현재 등록된 블랙리스트")
    table.insert(BlacklistUIElements, titleLabel)

    if #ChatBlacklist == 0 then
        local emptyLabel = BlacklistTab:CreateLabel("블랙 리스트에 추가될경우 제작자 한정으로 본닉과 찐닉을 전송합니다.")
        table.insert(BlacklistUIElements, emptyLabel)
    else
        for _, bannedName in ipairs(ChatBlacklist) do
            local userLabel = BlacklistTab:CreateLabel("🚫 " .. bannedName)
            table.insert(BlacklistUIElements, userLabel)
        end
    end
end

RefreshBlacklistUI()

local function ProcessBlacklistCommand(message)
    if string.sub(message, 1, 1) == ";" then
        local targetSearchName = string.sub(message, 2)
        if targetSearchName == "" then return end

        local foundPlayer = nil
        
        for _, v in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
            if string.find(string.lower(v.Name), string.lower(targetSearchName)) then
                foundPlayer = v
                break
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer then
            local realName = foundPlayer.Name
            
            if not table.find(ChatBlacklist, realName) then
                table.insert(ChatBlacklist, realName)
                
                Rayfield:Notify({
                    Title = "블랙리스트 설정 완료",
                    Content = "블랙리스트 " .. realName .. "으로 설정완료되었습니다",
                    Duration = 5,
                    Image = 4483362458
                })

                RefreshBlacklistUI()
            else
                Rayfield:Notify({
                    Title = "알림",
                    Content = "이미 블랙리스트에 등록된 유저입니다.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        else
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "등록 실패",
                Content = "서버에서 '" .. targetSearchName .. "' 유저를 찾을 수 없습니다.",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
end

pcall(function()
    game:GetService("TextChatService").MessageReceived:Connect(function(textChatMessage)
        if textChatMessage.TextSource then
            local sender = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayerByUserId(textChatMessage.TextSource.UserId)
            if sender == game.Players.LocalPlayer then
                ProcessBlacklistCommand(textChatMessage.Text)
            end
        end
    end)
end)

game.Players.LocalPlayer.Chatted:Connect(function(message)
    ProcessBlacklistCommand(message)
end)

-- =============================================================================
-- [ 블랙리스트 해제 
-- =============================================================================
BlacklistTab:CreateInput({
    Name = "블랙리스트 제거",
    PlaceholderText = "유저 닉네임 입력...",
    RemoveTextAfterFocusLost = true,
    Callback = function(Text)
        if not Text or Text == "" then return end
        
        local foundPlayer = nil
        for _, v in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if string.find(string.lower(v.Name), string.lower(Text)) then
                foundPlayer = v
                break
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer then
            local realName = foundPlayer.Name
            local displayName = foundPlayer.DisplayName
            local index = table.find(ChatBlacklist, realName)
            
            if index then
                table.remove(ChatBlacklist, index)
                RefreshBlacklistUI()
            end
            
            local currentTime = os.date("%X")
            
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "블랙리스트 해제 완료",
                Content = "@" .. realName .. "(" .. displayName .. ") 블랙리스트에 해제 되었습니다[ " .. currentTime .. " ]",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
            
            task.spawn(function()
                local label1 = BlacklistTab:CreateLabel("@" .. realName .. "본닉")
                local label2 = BlacklistTab:CreateLabel(displayName .. " 블랙리스트에 해제 되었습니다[ " .. currentTime .. " ]")
                
                task.wait(10)
                pcall(function() label1:Destroy() end)
                pcall(function() label2:Destroy() end)
            end)
        else
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "오류",
                Content = "서버에서 해당 유저를 찾을 수 없습니다...",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
    end
})

cmdWindowTab:CreateSection("Console Status")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("명령어 작동중✅")

cmdWindowTab:CreateSection("Command List")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("1. ;network owner = \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("2. ;bring \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("3. ;fling \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("4. ;unfling")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("5. ;view \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("6. ;unview")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("7. ;tppos \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("8. ;freeze \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("9. ;unfreeze \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("10.;goto \"PlayerName\"")
cmdWindowTab:CreateLabel("11.;kicklogs or ;kl")
local function getTargetPlayer(namePart)
    if not namePart or namePart == "" then return nil end
    local cleanPart = namePart:lower():gsub('"', ""):gsub("%s+", "")
    for _, p in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if string.find(p.Name:lower(), cleanPart) then
            return p
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function runChatCommand(msg)
    if msg:sub(1, 1) ~= ";" then return end
    
    local cleanMsg = msg:sub(2)
    
    if cleanMsg:sub(1, 14) == "network owner " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(15)
        local targetName = targetStr:match('=%s*"([^"]+)"') or targetStr:match("=%s*(.-)$")
        if targetName then
            local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetName)
            if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local hrp = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(hrp, hrp.CFrame)
                Rayfield:Notify({
                    Title = "Network Owner",
                    Content = "네트워크 오너가 " .. targetPlr.Name .. "으로 설정되었습니다.",
                    Duration = 5,
                    Image = 4483362458
                })
            end
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 6) == "bring " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(7)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local tHrp = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            local myHrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(tHrp, tHrp.CFrame)
            task.wait(0.05)
            tHrp.CFrame = myHrp.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -3)
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Bring",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님을 소환했습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 6) == "fling " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(7)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            _G.FlingTargetPlayer = targetPlr
            _G.FlingLoopActive = true
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Fling Start",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님에게 플링을 시작합니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
            task.spawn(function()
                while _G.FlingLoopActive and _G.FlingTargetPlayer == targetPlr do
                    pcall(function()
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(9999, 9999, 9999)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        end
                        pcall(function() game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true end)
                    end)
                    task.wait()
                end
            end)
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg == "unfling" then
        _G.FlingLoopActive = false
        _G.FlingTargetPlayer = nil
        pcall(function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            end
        end)
        Rayfield:Notify({
            Title = "Fling Stop",
            Content = "플링을 중지했습니다.",
            Duration = 5,
            Image = 4483362458
        })
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 5) == "view " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(6)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = targetPlr.Character.Humanoid
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "View",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님을 관전합니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg == "unview" then
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Unview",
                Content = "시점을 원래대로 돌렸습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 6) == "tppos " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(7)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0)
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Teleport",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님 위치로 텔레포트했습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 7) == "freeze " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(8)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local tHrp = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(tHrp, tHrp.CFrame)
            task.wait(0.05)
            tHrp.Anchored = true
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Freeze",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님을 고정했습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
        
    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 9) == "unfreeze " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(10)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local tHrp = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GrabEvents.SetNetworkOwner:FireServer(tHrp, tHrp.CFrame)
            task.wait(0.05)
            tHrp.Anchored = false
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Unfreeze",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님의 고정을 해제했습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end

    elseif cleanMsg:sub(1, 5) == "goto " then
        local targetStr = cleanMsg:sub(6)
        local targetPlr = getTargetPlayer(targetStr)
        if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
            Rayfield:Notify({
                Title = "Goto",
                Content = targetPlr.Name .. "님에게 이동했습니다.",
                Duration = 5,
                Image = 4483362458
            })
        end
    end
end

game.Players.LocalPlayer.Chatted:Connect(runChatCommand)
local KickLogs = {}
local KickLogUI = nil

local function ShowKickLogs()
    if KickLogUI then 
        KickLogUI:Destroy()
        KickLogUI = nil 
    end

    local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    ScreenGui.Name = "KickLogsUI"
    ScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    ScreenGui.Parent = game.CoreGui

    local MainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 440, 0, 400)
    MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -220, 0.5, -200)
    MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(18, 18, 22)
    MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    MainFrame.Parent = ScreenGui

    local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 14)
    UICorner.Parent = MainFrame

    local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 60, 60)
    Stroke.Thickness = 2
    Stroke.Parent = MainFrame

    
    local Title = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    Title.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 55)
    Title.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    Title.Text = "🚫 킥로그"
    Title.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
    Title.TextSize = 20
    Title.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    Title.Parent = MainFrame

    
    local CloseBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    CloseBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 36, 0, 36)
    CloseBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -42, 0, 10)
    CloseBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 40, 40)
    CloseBtn.Text = "×"
    CloseBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    CloseBtn.TextSize = 26
    CloseBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    CloseBtn.Parent = MainFrame

    local CloseCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    CloseCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
    CloseCorner.Parent = CloseBtn

    CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ScreenGui:Destroy()
        KickLogUI = nil
    end)

    
    local Scrolling = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
    Scrolling.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 1, -80)
    Scrolling.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 65)
    Scrolling.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    Scrolling.ScrollBarThickness = 5
    Scrolling.ScrollBarImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80)
    Scrolling.Parent = MainFrame

    local ListLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    ListLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    ListLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 8)
    ListLayout.Parent = Scrolling

    if #KickLogs == 0 then
        local Empty = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Empty.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 50)
        Empty.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Empty.Text = "아직 기록된 킥이 없습니다."
        Empty.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 120, 120)
        Empty.TextSize = 16
        Empty.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        Empty.Parent = Scrolling
    else
        for i, playerName in ipairs(KickLogs) do
            local Item = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            Item.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 38)
            Item.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 35)
            Item.Text = i .. ".  " .. playerName
            Item.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
            Item.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            Item.TextSize = 15
            Item.Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold
            Item.Parent = Scrolling

            local ItemCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
            ItemCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
            ItemCorner.Parent = Item

            local Padding = Instance.new("UIPadding")
            Padding.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 14)
            Padding.Parent = Item
        end
    end

    Scrolling.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, ListLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 30)
    KickLogUI = ScreenGui
end


game.Players.LocalPlayer.Chatted:Connect(function(msg)
    if msg:lower() == ";kicklogs" or msg:lower() == ";kl" then
        ShowKickLogs()
    end
end)
TargetTab:CreateLabel("맨위에 왼쪽에 돋보기 옆을 누르고 쭉 내리면 ui설정하는곳이 있습니다.")



local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local isLoopLagEnabled = false
local animSpeedValue = 1

task.spawn(function()
    while true do
        task.wait(0.1)
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                local animator = humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass("Animator")
                if animator then
                    for _, track in ipairs(animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                        if string.find(string.lower(track.Name), "walk") or string.find(string.lower(track.Name), "run") then
                            track:AdjustSpeed(animSpeedValue)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

playerTab:CreateInput({
   Name = "걷기 모션 속도",
   PlaceholderText = "0 \~ 5000 입력",
   RemoveTextAfterFocusLost = false,
   Callback = function(Text)
      local num = tonumber(Text)
      if num then
          animSpeedValue = num
      end
   end,
})

playerTab:CreateToggle({
   Name = "무한루프 방지 (리스폰 렉)",
   CurrentValue = false,
   Flag = "LagToggle",
   Callback = function(Value)
      isLoopLagEnabled = Value
   end,
})

player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    if isLoopLagEnabled then
        task.spawn(function()
            local start = tick()
            while tick() - start < 2.5 do
                math.random(1, 1000000) 
            end
        end)
    end
end)

player.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function()
    if isLoopLagEnabled then
        local start = tick()
        while tick() - start < 1.5 do
            math.random(1, 1000)
        end
    end
end)

local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer

local countryLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("서버 국가: 로딩중...")

task.spawn(function()
    local LocalizationService = game:GetService("LocalizationService")
    local success, code = pcall(function()
        return LocalizationService:GetCountryRegionForPlayerAsync(plr)
    end)
    
    local finalCode = (success and code) and code:upper() or "US"
    local name = "미국 (USA)"
    local emoji = "🇺🇸 "
    
    if finalCode == "KR" then name = "대한민국 (South Korea)" emoji = "🇰🇷 "
    elseif finalCode == "JP" then name = "일본 (Japan)" emoji = "🇯🇵 "
    elseif finalCode == "IN" then name = "인도 (India)" emoji = "🇮🇳 "
    elseif finalCode == "SG" then name = "싱가포르 (Singapore)" emoji = "🇸🇬 "
    elseif finalCode == "HK" then name = "홍콩 (Hong Kong)" emoji = "🇭🇰 "
    elseif finalCode == "TW" then name = "대만 (Taiwan)" emoji = "🇹🇼 "
    elseif finalCode == "CN" then name = "중국 (China)" emoji = "🇨🇳 "
    elseif finalCode == "US" then name = "미국 (USA)" emoji = "🇺🇸 "
    elseif finalCode == "GB" then name = "영국 (UK)" emoji = "🇬🇧 "
    elseif finalCode == "DE" then name = "독일 (Germany)" emoji = "🇩🇪 "
    elseif finalCode == "FR" then name = "프랑스 (France)" emoji = "🇫🇷 "
    elseif finalCode == "VN" then name = "베트남 (Vietnam)" emoji = "🇻🇳 "
    elseif finalCode == "TH" then name = "태국 (Thailand)" emoji = "🇹🇭 "
    elseif finalCode == "PH" then name = "필리핀 (Philippines)" emoji = "🇵🇭 "
    elseif finalCode == "MY" then name = "말레이시아 (Malaysia)" emoji = "🇲🇾 "
    elseif finalCode == "ID" then name = "인도네시아 (Indonesia)" emoji = "🇮🇩 "
    elseif finalCode == "AU" then name = "호주 (Australia)" emoji = "🇦🇺 "
    elseif finalCode == "CA" then name = "캐나다 (Canada)" emoji = "🇨🇦 "
    elseif finalCode == "BR" then name = "브라질 (Brazil)" emoji = "🇧🇷 "
    elseif finalCode == "RU" then name = "러시아 (Russia)" emoji = "🇷🇺 "
    elseif finalCode == "NL" then name = "네덜란드 (Netherlands)" emoji = "🇳🇱 "
    elseif finalCode == "TR" then name = "튀르키예 (Turkey)" emoji = "🇹🇷 "
    elseif finalCode == "MX" then name = "멕시코 (Mexico)" emoji = "🇲🇽 "
    elseif finalCode == "AE" then name = "아랍에미리트 (UAE)" emoji = "🇦🇪 "
    else
        name = "기타 국가 (" .. finalCode .. ")"
        pcall(function()
            local c1 = finalCode:sub(1,1):byte() + 127397
            local c2 = finalCode:sub(2,2):byte() + 127397
            emoji = utf8.char(c1) .. utf8.char(c2) .. " "
        end)
    end
    
    countryLabel:Set("서버 국가: " .. emoji .. name)
end)

local playerNameLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("플레이어: 로딩중...")
local executorLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("실행자: 로딩중...")
local ipLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("IP 주소: 로딩중...")
local exploitLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("실행기: 로딩중...")
local gameNameLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("게임: 로딩중...")
local userIdLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("유저 ID: 로딩중...")
local placeIdLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("게임 ID: 로딩중...")

task.spawn(function()
    playerNameLabel:Set("플레이어: " .. plr.DisplayName .. " (@" .. plr.Name .. ")")
    executorLabel:Set("실행자: " .. plr.DisplayName .. " (@" .. plr.Name .. ")")
    
    local success, ipResult = pcall(function()
        return game:HttpGet("no")
    end)
    if success then
        ipLabel:Set("IP 주소: " .. ipResult)
    else
        ipLabel:Set("IP 주소: 실패(주소 삭제됨)")
    end
    
    local exploitName = (identifyexecutor and identifyexecutor()) or (getexecutorname and getexecutorname()) or "Unknown Exploit"
    exploitLabel:Set("실행기: " .. exploitName)
    
    userIdLabel:Set("유저 ID: " .. plr.UserId)
    
    local marketSuccess, marketResult = pcall(function()
        return game:GetService("MarketplaceService"):GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId).Name
    end)
    if marketSuccess then
        gameNameLabel:Set("게임: " .. marketResult)
    else
        gameNameLabel:Set("게임: 정보 불러오기 실패")
    end
    
    placeIdLabel:Set("게임 ID: " .. game.PlaceId)
end)

local deviceLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("기기: 로딩중...")
local hwidLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("HWID: 로딩중...")
local pingLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("핑: 로딩중...")
local fpsLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("FPS: 로딩중...")
local accountAgeLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("계정 생성일 수: 로딩중...")
local membershipLabel = HubTab:CreateLabel("프리미엄 여부: 로딩중...")

local userInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local deviceType = "PC"
if userInputService.TouchEnabled and not userInputService.KeyboardEnabled then
    deviceType = "Mobile"
elseif userInputService.GamepadEnabled and not userInputService.KeyboardEnabled then
    deviceType = "Console"
end
deviceLabel:Set("기기: " .. deviceType)

local hwid = (gethwid and gethwid()) or "지원하지 않음"
hwidLabel:Set("HWID: " .. hwid)

accountAgeLabel:Set("계정 생성일 수: " .. plr.AccountAge .. "일")
membershipLabel:Set("프리미엄 여부: " .. (plr.MembershipType == Enum.MembershipType.Premium and "Yes" or "No"))

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(1) do
        local ping = game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValueString()
        pingLabel:Set("핑: " .. string.split(ping, " ")[1] .. "ms")
    end
end)

task.spawn(function()
    local runService = game:GetService("RunService")
    while true do
        local startTime = os.clock()
        runService.RenderStepped:Wait()
        local fps = math.floor(1 / (os.clock() - startTime))
        fpsLabel:Set("FPS: " .. fps)
        task.wait(0.3)
    end
end)
